File Under Ska is back!

File Under Ska has been a radio show at the Freies Radio für Stuttgart since June 2003.
We play both kinds - Ska and Rocksteady.

Since 2022, File Under Ska has been a part of the Suchtstation für Music-Junkies and is therefore listed under that name in the radio timetable.

Next shows: 16.01.2026, 20.02.2026, 20.03.2026, 17.04.2026, 22.06.2026, 19.06.2026 (Friday, 8 pm till 10 pm)

99,2 MHz in Stuttgart, Livestream: streaming.fueralle.org/frs-hi.mp3

Like our Facebook page to stay up to date.

The Homepage until 2017     The WordPress site until 2019

Check out the playlists from 770 shows below.

Upcoming concerts in and around Stuttgart:

  • Mi, 14.01.2026: Dreadskin Kick Box, Ritterstüble
  • Sa, 17.01.2026: Skaos, Mofos, Alte Mühle Filderstadt
  • Sa, 07.02.2026: The Nite Steadies, Peña Real Madrid
  • Fr, 06.03.2026: The Movement, Nerves, Goldmark's
  • Sa, 14.03.2026: The Nite Steadies, Cafe Eisele (Köngen)
  • Do, 30.04.2026: The Nite Steadies, Fellbacher Hopf im Kunstverein-Keller

Also check out motorcityrock.de, Trash-A-Go-Go!, stuttgigs.de, lift-online.de/veranstaltungen/konzerte and gig-blog.net
